And they further – further, the point was that if and when they would be used, they would brief Congress at that time"<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129"><a href="#cite_note-129">[129]</a></sup> Pelosi's office stated that she later protested the technique and that she concurred with objections raised by Democratic colleague <a href="/wiki/Jane_Harman" title="Jane Harman">Jane Harman</a> in a letter to the <a href="/wiki/Central_Intelligence_Agency" title="Central Intelligence Agency">CIA</a> in early 2003.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NYT_Hero_118-1"><a href="#cite_note-NYT_Hero-118">[118]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="On_President_Bush">On President Bush</span></h3>
<p>In mid-July 2008, two days after President <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> stated that Congress was ineffective and said, "This is not a record to be proud of, and I think the American people deserve better",<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-failure_130-0"><a href="#cite_note-failure-130">[130]</a></sup> Pelosi responded by calling the president "a total failure, losing all credibility with the American people on the war, on the economy, on energy, you name the subject" and that Congress had been "sweeping up after his mess over and over and over again".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-failure_130-1"><a href="#cite_note-failure-130">[130]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Electoral_history">Electoral history</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nancy_pelosi_drive.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2680" data-file-width="3928" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Nancy_pelosi_drive.JPG/220px-Nancy_pelosi_drive.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Nancy_pelosi_drive.JPG/330px-Nancy_pelosi_drive.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Nancy_pelosi_drive.JPG/440px-Nancy_pelosi_drive.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Nancy_pelosi_drive.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The city of <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco" title="San Francisco">San Francisco</a> named a street in <a href="/wiki/Golden_Gate_Park" title="Golden Gate Park">Golden Gate Park</a> in honor of Pelosi after her many years representing the city in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Congress" title="U.S. Congress">Congress</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Electoral_history_of_Nancy_Pelosi" title="Electoral history of Nancy Pelosi">Electoral history of Nancy Pelosi</a></div>
<p>Pelosi's only close race so far has been the special election to succeed Sala Burton's seat after her death in February 1987. In the special election's Democratic primary, Pelosi narrowly defeated San Francisco Supervisor <a href="/wiki/Harry_Britt" title="Harry Britt">Harry Britt</a>, considered the more "progressive" candidate, with 36 percent of the vote to his 32 percent.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nationnewface_15-1"><a href="#cite_note-nationnewface-15">[15]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup> In the runoff against Republican candidate Harriet Ross, Pelosi received more than a 2-to-1 majority of votes cast in a turnout that comprised about 24% of eligible voters.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132"><a href="#cite_note-132">[132]</a></sup> Since then, Pelosi has enjoyed overwhelming support in her political career, collecting 76 and 77 percent of the vote in <a href="/wiki/California%27s_5th_congressional_district" title="California's 5th congressional district">California's 5th congressional district</a> for the 1988 and 1990 Race for U.S. House of Representatives. In 1992, after the redistricting from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Census,_1990" title="United States Census, 1990">1990 Census</a>, Pelosi ran in <a href="/wiki/California%27s_8th_congressional_district" title="California's 8th congressional district">California's 8th congressional district</a>, which now covered the San Francisco area. She has continued to post landslide victories since, dropping beneath 80 percent of the vote only twice.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_background">Personal background</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span></h3>
<p>Her husband, since 1963, is <a href="/wiki/Paul_Pelosi" title="Paul Pelosi">Paul Pelosi</a>. They have five children: Nancy Corinne, <a href="/wiki/Christine_Pelosi" title="Christine Pelosi">Christine</a>, Jacqueline, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Paul_Pelosi,_Jr." title="Paul Pelosi, Jr.">Paul</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Alexandra_Pelosi" title="Alexandra Pelosi">Alexandra</a>, as well as eight grandchildren. Alexandra, a journalist, covered the Republican presidential campaigns in 2000 and made a film about the experience, <i><a href="/wiki/Journeys_with_George" title="Journeys with George">Journeys with George</a></i>. In 2007, Christine published a book, <i>Campaign Boot Camp: Basic Training for Future Leaders</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup></p>
<p>Pelosi lives in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific_Heights,_San_Francisco,_California" title="Pacific Heights, San Francisco, California">Pacific Heights</a> neighborhood of San Francisco.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Financial_status">Financial status</span></h3>
<p>Nancy Pelosi is among the richest members of Congress,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-richest_134-0"><a href="#cite_note-richest-134">[134]</a></sup> with an estimated net worth of approximately $58 million, the 12th highest estimated net worth in Congress, according to the nonpartisan <a href="/wiki/Center_for_Responsive_Politics" title="Center for Responsive Politics">Center for Responsive Politics</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135"><a href="#cite_note-135">[135]</a></sup></p>
<p>While members of Congress are not required to disclose their exact net worth, organizations such as the <a href="/wiki/Center_for_Responsive_Politics" title="Center for Responsive Politics">Center for Responsive Politics</a> prepare estimated ranges based on public disclosures. The CRP's midpoint estimate of the Pelosis' net worth is $58,436,537 as of 2009, the most recent year for which figures are available, with a possible range from $7 million to $124 million.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136"><a href="#cite_note-136">[136]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Involvement_in_Italian-American_community">Involvement in Italian-American community</span></h3>
<p>Pelosi is a board member of the <a href="/wiki/National_Organization_of_Italian_American_Women" title="National Organization of Italian American Women">National Organization of Italian American Women</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup> Additionally, Pelosi served for 13 years as a board member of the <a href="/wiki/National_Italian_American_Foundation" title="National Italian American Foundation">National Italian American Foundation</a> (NIAF). In 2007, she received the NIAF Special Achievement Award for Public Advocacy and continues to be involved in the Foundation today.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honors_and_decorations">Honors and decorations</span></h2>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1500" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/23px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/35px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/45px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a> <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ITA_OMRI_2001_GC_BAR.svg"><img alt="ITA OMRI 2001 GC BAR.svg" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="218" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/ITA_OMRI_2001_GC_BAR.svg/55px-ITA_OMRI_2001_GC_BAR.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/ITA_OMRI_2001_GC_BAR.svg/84px-ITA_OMRI_2001_GC_BAR.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/ITA_OMRI_2001_GC_BAR.svg/109px-ITA_OMRI_2001_GC_BAR.svg.png 2x" width="55"/></a> Knight Grand Cross of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merit_of_the_Italian_Republic" title="Order of Merit of the Italian Republic">Order of Merit of the Italian Republic</a> on June 2, 2007<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138"><a href="#cite_note-138">[138]</a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9e/Flag_of_Japan.svg/23px-Flag_of_Japan.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9e/Flag_of_Japan.svg/35px-Flag_of_Japan.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9e/Flag_of_Japan.svg/45px-Flag_of_Japan.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:JPN_Kyokujitsu-sho_1Class_BAR.svg" title="ribbon bar"><img alt="ribbon bar" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="218" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/JPN_Kyokujitsu-sho_1Class_BAR.svg/59px-JPN_Kyokujitsu-sho_1Class_BAR.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/JPN_Kyokujitsu-sho_1Class_BAR.svg/89px-JPN_Kyokujitsu-sho_1Class_BAR.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/JPN_Kyokujitsu-sho_1Class_BAR.svg/118px-JPN_Kyokujitsu-sho_1Class_BAR.svg.png 2x" width="59"/></a> Grand Cordon of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Rising_Sun" title="Order of the Rising Sun">Order of the Rising Sun</a> on April 29, 2015</li>
<li>In 2006 she was named <a href="/wiki/Barbara_Walters" title="Barbara Walters">Barbara Walters</a>' <a href="/wiki/Barbara_Walters%27_10_Most_Fascinating_People" title="Barbara Walters' 10 Most Fascinating People">Most Fascinating Person</a> of the year.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139"><a href="#cite_note-139">[139]</a></sup></li>
<li>She has been listed numerous times on <i>Forbes</i> list of the world's 100 most powerful women. As of 2014, Pelosi was ranked 26th.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Forbes14_140-0"><a href="#cite_note-Forbes14-140">[140]</a></sup></li>
